I thought that sense I will be keeping my Nissan Pathfinder for a long time, this sounded like a great deal.  I recently had some suspension work done on my Nissan Pathfinder and needed to get the tires aligned again.  First time I went in for the alignment, everything looked good but in about 12 hours my tires were so crooked!  Went back in again and asked them to do it again.  They did and again the alignment lasted about 12 hours.  This time, my tires went out so bad lights on my dash started going off.  Once again, back to the shop for another alignment.  I asked them how tight they were making the camber bolts because that is what was causing my tires to go out of alignment.  They only told me that they do it to spec.  Once again, they realigned the tires but after 12 hours everything was back to a horrible condition.  After 3 times going in and no luck in properly doing an alignment they told me they think some bushing in my suspension was broken and that was causing the problem.  They said the bolts are not moving but the bushing are so bad that they need to be replaced.  I didn't believe that for one second because I just did some suspension work done on the car and many parts are brand new.  I also noticed that in the small time I drove around within the 3 alignments and my tires being so far out of alignment my back two, almost new tires, have significant bad tire wear from the inside to the outside. I went over to America Tire Company right down the street and they told me they have never seen such a horrible alignment job. <Date>1571769714502<//Date>< review>
Arrive early for close and in-front parking spots or else have to park farther in the back of building.
Today, 22-Oct-2019, I arrived at 6:15am and I'm the first and also the first in-line too.
Door opened at 8am as promised.
Got my initial form and filled it out.
They just waited 5 minutes more for our fifth early guests to completed our form then called us up in a group of 5 at a time.
Then we were called up individually by our numbers and this time, they verify our appointment letter and date-stamp it.
We then are sent to another final lobby room to sit and wait for our picture and "index & middle finger" prints.
Done!
Filled out my little yellow customer service survey, dropped it into one of the 3 boxes, and then EXIT at the double-door just left of the table where those 3 boxes were.
Walked over to my car, parked facing Magnolia Ave, sat in the driver's seat, started the engine, looked at the clock on my dashboard, it's 8:15am ü§óü§óü§ó
So again, if you wish for speedy services here like how I experienced it, ARRIVE early üòãüòâüòé
Peace, and I'm out...until 10-years later üòéüòéüòé<//review>

< Review>
I haven't been there for a long time.  I was pleasantly surprised
It's very clean and Martin the bartender/server was knowledgeable and friendly. I had the Sunday special which is fried chicken with mashed potatoes and gravy and broccoli. It was good.  A person at my table was happy with the fish and chips.  The other person at my table had the burger and fries.  Got a definite thumbs up on that. They have a special every night except for Friday when they have music. The prices are good.   My chicken dinner was only $12.99.  On Saturday they have prime rib for $13.99.  You can sit inside or outside and watch the golfers.  There are fire pits out there so I definitely want to give that a try.  They also have breakfast all day.  Nice place to bring visitors or just go to a pleasant, quiet place to dine.  Give it a try.< /Review>

First visit was fine. Ordered the gyro and enjoyed it with no issues. Second visit was a bit more frustrating. Ordered chicken shawarma and sat down to wait. Staff dropped it off to the adjacent table who ordered after me even after making an attempt to let them know they are dropping my plate off to the wrong table. I let the staff know at the front that I believe they made a mistake, no big deal.

Front staff says "Oh no worries there is another one coming up." Cool, guess I'll wait a little longer. Sit back down and a few minutes later staff is bringing more food to the table next to me, the same one that ordered after me. Keep in mind they are a larger party. I'm just here on my lunch break trying to eat and get back to work. Feels bad to see a large party get served before a single order especially since they came in after I did.

This table looks at the food they're brought and say "Hey, I ordered the kebab not the shawarma." Hmm... I'm still patiently waiting, hoping they bring me my food soon. Staff starts heading my way, drops off chicken kebab, and says "Hey you were right, I accidentally gave your food to the other table." This is the part that kind of turned the whole thing sour, the gentlemen helping me turns around to walk back to the counter after acknowledging he gave my order away and then dropping off the other tables order in front of me. I had to stop him and ask if I could get the order I wanted.

Best part here, after waiting even longer, they bring my order out... to the other table.

< Text>
This place is fine. I mean, it's Little Caesars. It's fast-food pizza and if you expect anything more than that then you should rethink your life choices. If you're in a hurry and need pizza fast, this is your place. Their pizza is perfectly fine and tasty. Their non-regular items, like the bacon deep-dish, are actually really good. I wish they would have them year-round.

I just tried their Hawaiian pizza for the first time because usually I just get a hot-n-ready pepperoni, and I really liked that too. I think it actually think it can rival some of the other major chains as well.

Don't be afraid to mix it up sometimes.

The only reason to avoid this particular location would be because it is a transient hub and 9 times out of 10 you're guaranteed to be asked for changed by some dudes just hanging out outside.< /Text>
